Let the blood flow freely and squeeze the wound with your hand or some other object until bleeding stops. If bleeding from the incision of an artery or vein hinders you, cauterize it until the bleeding stops. Then treat the wound with other remedies until it is healed.
de ydropisie	Of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer: si est eclites soulement; et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces .ij. semblances: c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose; donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses; si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance; et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	We have already spoken in the section on the signs of dropsy and how water is collected in it, and the signs of each kind and their treatment by medicines and surgery. Only in one kind called "eclites" should surgery be considered. One must not perform surgery on these two kinds: tympanites and yposarche, as they are deadly conditions. Therefore, if you treat dropsy called "eclites" with medicine and it does not improve, examine whether the patient is weak or has another disease such as tympanites or diarrhea. If the patient is strong and healthy and has no other diseases besides dropsy, and is not too young or too old, then one should perform surgery in this way:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme: Et soit trenchans de .ij. pars. a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	Lift the patient up onto your hands, and have an assistant press the abdomen from below using the lower part of the foot. Then take a spinal needle shaped like this: it should be sharp at both ends but not so sharp that it can reach the intestines when inserted, nor so blunt that it cannot cut.
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines: si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude .iij. dois droit desoz sus lou poignil; et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude .iij. dois; et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	Then check if the dropsy has spread towards the intestines: you should cut through the flesh about three fingers' width below the navel. If the dropsy is due to liver disease, make your incision on the left side of the navel; if it's due to bile, make it on the right side. Make sure the patient does not lie on the incision so that the superfluous fluid does not drain into a weak area.
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor; puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme: Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz .i. petit pertus; et ou costeit d’une part, .iij. pertus; et .ij. d’autre part, et .i. d’autre; et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	Then pierce the skin with the needle and insert it, lifting your hand so that the needle goes between the skin and the fascia about the width of a nail or around four fingers' width. Pierce the fascia until you reach the empty space where the water is located. Then insert this instrument shaped like a silver tube: it should be made of bronze or lightweight brass with a small hole at one end and three holes on one side and two on the other. The edges should be cut like a feather, as shown in the illustration of how writers shape their quills.
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument; vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	At the top of this instrument is the alembic (a container with a long neck). When the instrument reaches the water, tilt it downwards to collect about half or a third of the fluid. Do not remove too much at once as this could cause the patient to die from loss of spirit, faintness, or approaching death due to excessive bleeding.
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz; puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere; puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	But remove the fluid according to the patient's strength and their pulse rate. Then withdraw the instrument and retain the fluid using your hand over the hole in the fascia that you pierced earlier. Resume draining on the following day if the patient tolerates it well, removing only a small amount of fluid each time.
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue. Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre; et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	Continue this process for a few days until only a little water remains. If you are unsure about the patient's condition and leave too much fluid, treat them with warm baths, poultices or sun exposure, and give them dry medicines to drink. Also cauterize the stomach, liver, and spleen after draining the fluid, as I have described previously.
de l’estopement de la verge	The section on impotence is titled "De l'estopement de la verge" which means "On the stoppage of the penis". This refers to erectile dysfunction or impotence. The text discusses the causes and treatments for this condition.
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu. Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout .i. spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme: puis met ou pertus .i. clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi .iij. jors ou iiij. et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet; et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	Sometimes children are born without a urethral opening or with a small one, or it may not be in its proper position. In such cases, it is necessary to pierce the penis with a very fine needle shaped like this: then insert a thin silver catheter and tie it off, leaving it in place for three or four days. When the child needs to urinate, remove the catheter and allow them to do so. Then replace the catheter. Sometimes no catheter may be needed as urine will still flow around the closed opening.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera. Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut; et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	Those whose urethral opening is small will benefit from treatment with a silver catheter as described above, which will help to widen the opening. Those born without a urethral opening at its proper location are disabled and cannot urinate properly until they learn to lift their penis upwards. They also have difficulty impregnating women because semen cannot reach the mouth of the womb (cervix). This is considered a serious condition.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient; et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	The technique for performing a circumcision is as follows: have the patient lie on their back. Then grasp the glans of the penis and cut it around like the tip of a feather quill so that the urethral opening remains in its proper position. Be careful not to cause bleeding, which can occur frequently during this procedure. If bleeding does occur, use something that stops bleeding and treat any resulting wound until it has healed.
des pustules de la verge	Of the blisters of the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide; et en i a malignes et non malignes; si covient que tu les preignes a .i. oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien; puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Often these blisters appear on the penis, and there is an ugly appearance of skin; and some are malignant and others benign. Therefore you must take them with tweezers, squeeze them out and clean all of them thoroughly, then put wet cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment; then apply the ointment diaphoretic until it is gone.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere. Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier; et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer. Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion; si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the blister is malignant, of foul color and stinking, then you must cauterize it. When you have squeezed it out, and if the blister is at the tip of the penis, and has part inside the skin and part outside, then you must remove the inner part first; and when that is healed, then cure the outer part. For when you cure them together, it is not certain that the glans of the penis will not be pierced, and blackness and corruption comes into its flesh and into the coition. Therefore you must cut away all that is black and corrupted, then bind on the wound with honey and flour paste made from the bark of pomegranate fruits and figs; then cure it with other dressings until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme: Li cauteres si aide as .ij. dispositions ensamble: c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption; et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi; et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a .i. estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	And if there is bleeding, then apply the lunar cautery according to this method: The cautery has two uses together: for bleeding and corruption. And if the glans of the penis is corrupted and retracted, then you must insert a lead pipe into the urethra and have the sick person urinate through it; and when the skin at the tip of the penis that needs to be circumcised is exposed, or it is exposed due to an injury or aposteme, then you must burn it with a sharp instrument until the foreskin is separated and the glans of the penis is delivered from all sides;
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a .i. spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil; puis dessevre belement entre .ij., et i met .i. subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	And if it is difficult to separate these parts, then you must burn them with one spatula at the tip of the penis and foreskin; then carefully dissect between two and insert a thin linen cloth soaked in cold water, so that it may not adhere again.
de la circoncision	Et se c’est un garcon qui doit estre circoncis, si covient que tu coupes le pelz a .vi. mois, et les autres enfans a .xii. mois; et il est bon quant tu les feras circonsire quant l’enfant aura .iii. ans ou environ.
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Circumcision is not like other wounds in its continuity; nevertheless, when we perform this operation willingly and especially on children, it is necessary that we do the best work with the least harm possible.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not practice circumcision on their children because it was not part of their law, and we only have knowledge of it through experimentation.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor .i. dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule; si fuioit li keurs car il i a .ij. toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	Because I have wanted the majority of masters and surgeons who perform circumcision around one dal, and by force, and for an entire novacule; so it was that the heart would flee because there are two tissues, and sometimes one cuts the upper one and leaves the lower one.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre; et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	Otherwise they cover it up and the pain is doubled, and at the time of cleansing the point of the member is not secure; and sometimes during cleansing of the foreskin the knife slips and ruins the operation, and many times it happens that they do not need cleansing, which I have seen.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Regarding the cleansing done by force, I have found that using a thread tied around the entire length is the best experiment because the force cuts equally well both above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en .i. tout soul tens; mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir; et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	"For when you press your hand thus, cut evenly in one continuous stroke; but ensure the thread is tightly wrapped around the skin. And the manner of the first operation should be such that you make the child think, if it understands, that you are only tying the thread around the staff and then allow it to enjoy all possible ways."
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens; puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens; puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz .i. poc a .i. autre liien; et la tien as .ij. dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les .ij. liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	"Then hold the staff upright between your hands and hide the force between your hands or beneath your feet so that the child does not see them nor any of the instruments. Then place your hand on the staff and blow gently, then pull upwards until the skin of the staff is entered. Then clean it well from the filth that has gathered there, then tie the opening with a double thread, then tie it below one knot to another. Hold it with two fingers at the second knot near the little finger and cut between the two knots, then quickly lift the heart upwards and pull out the tip of the staff."
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres; et met poudre sus et sus la poudre .i. drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	"Then allow the blood to flow freely until it stops, for this is the mother's part; then sprinkle powder on top of the powder and place a piece of gauze soaked in a mixture of raw egg yolk tempered with rosewater, boiled and cooled, mixed with good fresh rose oil. Leave it overnight and continue the treatment until it heals."
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste: li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	"The form of the instruments for cleansing should be as follows: the two tips should be thin and sharp, and the tips should also be as large as a hazelnut, equal in size:"
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision; donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme; et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	"The error of cleansing occurs when the heart is inside the incision, therefore it is necessary to extend it with your fingernail before the wound becomes inflamed; and cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, then use forceps, and then cut it."
Et s’il trespassent .iij. jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement; si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	"And if it lasts for three days and the part below the staff is swollen, let it be until the inflammation has subsided, then gently scrape off the scab; cut as much as you can move without harming the part of the staff, for it will not harm it."
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point; cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"Therefore treat the wound with quick-acting powder, as we have said when treating powders, and if you cut too much from the heart and it goes upwards, it will not harm. Treat it therefore as we have said until it heals."
dou retenement de l’urine	"On the retention of urine"
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	"The retention of urine is due to the obstruction of stone, or congealed blood, or bowel, or flesh, or similar things, which we have mentioned in the division:"
et se li urine n’est desliie, et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	"And if the urine is not flowing and you see that retention is due to a stone lodged in or near the neck of the bladder, then the patient should be bent over on their knees; place their feet on their back and extend their belly towards the back, and have the patient push down as hard as they can; thus the neck of the bladder will be forced open above for the expulsion of the stone, so that the urine is released."
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil; et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	"And if it does not come out as we have said and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer extraction with all the instruments called a 'syringe', of which this is the form: made of thin silver, like the feather of a bird; it should be one and a half palms long and thin at the tip."
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren .i. fil double, et lie au chief .i. poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue; et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	"And the method of issuing urine is as follows: take one doubled thread and tie a small bag of wool or cotton at its end, then insert the end of the thread into the syringe. Cut off any excess wool and push it all the way to the tip of the syringe. Then grease the syringe with oil or butter and dove's dung. Have the patient sit on a chair, raise their bladder and penis with moistened oil and olive oil water."
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude; puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors; puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	"Then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the penis. Then fold the penis upwards towards the belly and push the syringe forward until it reaches the bladder. The patient will feel when it is empty. If this is not done correctly, it may be because the tube through which it passes is twisted. Then pull out the thread with the wool bag attached, and the urine follows the wool. Finally, remove the syringe and allow the urine to flow."
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	"And continue using the syringe until the bladder is emptied, then relieve the patient."
des maladies de la vessie	"On the diseases of the bladder"
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	"When there is erosion or blood in the bladder, or putrefaction has accumulated there, and you see that watery and medicinal substances are being discharged, then use all the instruments called a 'clepsydra', of which this is the form:"
Elle est close, et si a .iij. pertus: .ij. d’une part, et .i. d’autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	"It is closed and has three holes: two on one side and one on the other, as you can see. The high parts are made such that medicinal substances will fit tightly without additional pressure being applied to close the penis, so that moisture can be drawn out and inserted as needed."
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens; si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	"And when you see that your medicinal substances are being discharged into the bladder, insert the tip of the catheter into the moisture and draw out what is inside. Then replace the catheter firmly; thus the moisture will enter and reach the bladder, so that the patient feels it."
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:	"And this is the form of the fine enema used to administer an enema to the bladder:"
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a .i. sein ou li liiens chiet; puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les .ij. seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe .i. poc celle moistor sus le feu; puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	"And it is made of silver or brass, with the tip higher and one loop below where it falls. Then take a bladder from a sheep and fill it with the moisture you wish to use for the enema. Tie it between the two loops with a doubled thread. Heat some of this moisture over the fire. Then insert the tip of the enema into the penis and press your hand on the bladder until you feel that the moisture has reached the bladder."
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai .i. cercle, et le perce rondement entor; puis boute .i. fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble .i. dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument; et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	"And if you do not have the bladder of a sheep, take a piece of parchment and make a circle from it. Pierce it roundly all around, then pass a strong thread through these holes, assemble the circle like a sieve, and put inside what you wish to use for oil, moisture, and water. Tie it with the instrument and proceed as you would with the bladder."
de la piere	"on stones"
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	"I have already discussed in the section on stones their different types and methods of extraction along with medicinal remedies. I also explained the difference between stones that enter through the rains and all the signs associated with them, as well as which stones require surgical intervention - both in the bladder and in the penis. I will now explain this briefly and clearly."
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont .iiij. ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	"I say that stones which enter the bladder occur most frequently in children. This is a sign that urine is being expelled from the bladder like water in its fineness. The child will strain and grind his penis and frequently urinate until it becomes painful. In many cases, this condition is accompanied by inflammation. Children under the age of four usually have an easy recovery, while older adults find it much more difficult. Those who are middle-aged fare moderately well. The cure is easier for those with large stones than for those with small ones."
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines. Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	And when we come to the treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient with a clyster to draw out all the foul matter that is in the intestines. For it sometimes hinders finding the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche ded ens;	Then take the patient by the feet and lay them downwards and move them towards the bottom so that the stone descends into the depths of the bladder, which sometimes rises to the high place; then have him sit between your hands prepared in this way, with his hands below his thighs, so that the bladder is completely inclined downward; then search for it and touch it inside;
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere. Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	If you feel the stone in the flank, then immediately cut on the stone. And if it does not fall out completely when touched, moisten your middle finger with oil from the left hand if the patient is a child, or your index finger if the patient is a youth; place it in its base and search for the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, grasp it at the neck of the bladder; then press on it with your finger and push it out where you saw cutting.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	And command the minister to press the bladder with his hand, and he commands that with his right hand he stretch the scrotum upwards, and with his left hand remove the skin that is beneath the scrotum in the part where the incision is made; then insert the spatula like this, which is its shape:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	And make the incision between what is between the scrotum and the fundament, not in the middle but on the left side of the groin; and let it be straight over the stone, and your two fingers should always be on the fundament, and let the cut be wide on this side, and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	Perhaps the pressure of your two fingers on the fundament will cause it to slip out without effort; and know that there are stones with angles and edges: these are difficult to remove; but there are also those that are smooth, round like a pebble, from which extraction is easy.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li .i. estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge .i. poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	Therefore, for those stones that have angles and edges, make the incision larger; and if it does not slip out, then you must extract it with forceps that are like a chisel at the end, in order to grasp the stone so that it does not escape; or place underneath one of these subtle curved instruments at the end; and if you cannot catch it this way, widen the hole by a little, and if the skin tears, apply vitriol
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors. Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie. Car .ij. choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	And if there are more than one stone, first remove the largest one at the neck of the bladder, then cut above it, then extract it and then remove the smaller ones if there are several. And if they are very large, then they must be removed and a larger incision made. For two things can happen to the patient: either he dies, or urine comes out continuously from where the wound cannot be closed; but nevertheless, make every effort to extract it, or crush it with forceps until you remove it in pieces
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus .i. drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	And once you have completed your task, fill the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, then compress it and place over it a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine, or in oil and rosewater and cold water, to soothe the hot inflammation; then wrap the patient in blankets up to his neck, and do not untie the bandage until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you remove the bandage, wash the wound area very well with oil and water, then apply ointment of diacereion and ointment of basilicon until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine: boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	And if hot inflammation comes to the wound and corrosion, and congealed blood appears in the bladder, and urine retention occurs, which is recognized by the fact that it does not flow out with urine: then insert your finger into the wound and extract that blood, for if any remains, it will harm the bladder and cause its corruption
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les .ij. cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	Then wash the wound with water and rosewater and salt, and help him in every way that you know until he is healed; and it is necessary that each time you treat him, you tie his two thighs together, and apply the medicines to the wound area
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure. Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	And if the stone is small and it is in the urethra and stuck there, preventing urine from flowing out; treat it as I said earlier, that you cut it many times, or excuse yourself from cutting by this treatment. I have already tested this method successfully
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take one iron needle according to this shape and with three points stuck into a splinter of wood
puis pren .i. fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge. Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	Then take one thread and tie it around the urethra below the stone so that it cannot go back into the bladder; then insert the needle gently into the urethra until it reaches the stone; then turn the needle slowly in the stone little by little until you can pierce the stone on the other side; then urine will soon come out, then press your hand on what remains of the stone that is inside the urethra. It will soon be crushed and come out with the urine, and the patient will be healed
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie .i. fil desoz la piere et .i. autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les .ij. liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, then tie one thread below the stone and another above it, then make an incision in the urethra at the location of the stone between the two threads, then extract it with forceps, and untie the thread, and clean the congealed blood that is in the wound; and treat it until it heals
de la piere des femmes	de la piere des femmes
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It rarely happens that a stone enters into women's urethra, and if it does happen sometimes, the treatment is difficult, and it is forbidden for three reasons: firstly, because by chance the woman may be a virgin; secondly, because one cannot find a woman who is well-informed and willing to uncover herself before physicians
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a.	And the third reason is that by chance one cannot find a woman who is skilled in this art of hands; and the fourth reason is that a woman's stone is deeper than a man's stone, which means that a deeper incision must be made, and there is great fear involved
Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier .i. caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	And if you are compelled to do this, then you must take a skilled midwife, and if you cannot find one, then search for a chaste virgin who knows something about this matter; and present her with a clean sheet suitable for examining women's lives, or a woman who knows part of the art, and command her to perform what you command regarding the examination of the stone
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And examine very carefully whether the woman is a virgin: if she is, then you must insert your finger into her fundament and search for the stone; and if you find it, constrain it with your finger from below, and command her to insert her finger into the patient's vagina and feel and press her left hand firmly on the bladder
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	If she finds it, then she must move it little by little from the entrance of the bladder until it reaches the root of the thigh; then make an incision on the stone at the root of the thigh opposite the middle of the vagina, where it is usually located, and feel the stone in that area; and do not move your finger above or below the stone, and make the first incision small
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains. si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	then insert the forceps into the incision, if you feel the stone so close to the wound that it can come out with forceps; and know that there are many types of stones: small and large, sharp and smooth, long and round, and those with roots. Know their appearances in order to determine the outcome
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	And if the urine flows abundantly, then put powdered vitriol in place and hold it for an hour until the urine is stanched; then return to your task until the stone is extracted, and have the instruments that I told you about regarding the extraction of stones from men ready to assist you
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if the blood begins to flow, and this is from an artery that has been cut, then apply powder to the spot and hold it with bandages and bindings, and do not recommence cutting again, and leave the stone alone and do not remove it, lest by chance the patient dies; then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has been stopped, and the place is ready, then return to your work until the stone is removed.
de hernie carnouse	of carnal hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	Aquatic hernia is nothing other than a gathering of moisture or white seed, which is under the skin of the thighs containing the egg; and it is called "seed," and sometimes properly in the fabric of the egg, so that one might think there is another egg; and this happens if not punctured.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this hernia comes from weakness that affects the thighs, and this matter becomes spread out.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the thighs, and this moisture has many colors: either declining towards yellowness, or without redness, or black, or aquatic white, and these things happen more often
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, .i. poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And these are the signs to recognize this gathering: for if it is in the white seed that we have spoken of, then the swelling is round, about the size of an egg's shape, and does not open the skin because it has moisture all around it.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in its own fabric, then the swelling is round with part of the egg, and for this reason one might think that it is another egg;
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	"Now if moisture is between the skin of the thighs and the white fat, it is clearly felt; therefore, when you see the color of the moisture, try the entire introite square, which has the form given above."
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	"Therefore, according to what comes after the introite, judge what is inside."
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	"And when we cauterize it with iron, then the patient must be made healthy according to their strength and the fullness of their body; then lay them on their back, on something slightly raised, and place many cloths beneath them;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des .ij. costelz dou keur des coions;	Then sit on his left side, and command the attendant to sit on the right side, extending the wand towards one of the two ribs on the left side of the heart.
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take the left spatula and cut through the skin of the thighs from the lengthwise until near the knee, and make your incision straight down through the skin to expose the white fascia. Then carefully peel it back according to your ability.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a .i. large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Then pierce the water-filled sac with one large opening and remove all the water. Then place your bandages, elevating the water-filled sac upwards. Do not touch the heart of the lungs, but only the water-filled sac itself. Cut away everything, or cut in pieces if necessary, from its sides subtly, so that if you do not cut it finely enough, the water will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les .ij. leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the egg jumps outside of your work, then return it to its place once you have completed the operation on the water-filled sac. Then join the two leaves of the heart of the lungs with a suture, and then treat it like other wounds until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the egg corrupted by another illness, then tie up the vessels that are suspended there, stopping the flow of blood. Then cut open the lung at all the suspensory ligaments and remove the egg, treating it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en .ij. parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont .ij. ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	And if water is gathered in two parts together, know that these are the roots of the lungs. Cut open the other part as you did with the first one equally, then suck out the blood and place moistened wool in rose oil on the wound
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les .ij. coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	Then place another piece of wool moistened in wine and oil on top of the two lungs, and cover them with doubled cloths. Then tie it all together according to this pattern:
Puis pren .ij. drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les .ij. angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	Then take two pieces of cloth and fill them with wool waste according to this pattern. Sew them together at the collar of the breeches, and one piece should be placed on the buttocks up to the back, while the other covers the front of the elbow. Then tie both ends over the two angles of the lungs, and all the ties should come together in a loop around the breeches.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes .i. cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	And sometimes this root is treated with a cautery instead of an iron cut, and thus you should take one scalpel-shaped cautery, cut through the skin of the lungs, and heat it as we have said so that the white sac containing water is exposed
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Then take the cautery in this manner and prick the white sac once with it, then burn it with this sharp cautery that is hot:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	"And cut in all ways that you can, until you scrape it all clean; and make sure the fire does not touch the eye; and know that this work is more sound; and move cautiously to avoid blood loss, and soften the edges of your incisions."
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	"And if anything goes against you, such as a wound that is hot or blood loss or any other issue, then treat what is going against you, according to what has been said before."
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai,	"And if the patient is fearful and does not wish to undergo this procedure due to its harshness, then prepare for perforation, as I shall tell you, and it is necessary that when you are certain through the signs that we have mentioned that watery humor is present there."
si fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege leveit; puis perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	"So make the patient sit on a high seat; then pierce the boil in the part below it with a wide-bladed scalpel, and insert the perforator along the length of the body; and let the opening be large enough for all the fluid to flow out."
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	"Then place cotton on the wound and tie it down, and leave it there for the remaining fluid to flow out, then treat it until the wound is healed."
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge .i. poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés .vj. mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	"And if the white cloth does not allow the fluid to flow out of the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a pen or the instrument used to treat watery humors, the shape of which is shown above; and widen the wound by one finger's breadth, and know that the fluid will return and gather again after five or six months, and when it has gathered as before, then the patient will pass his days."
de l’aposteme des coions	"On boils on buttocks"
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	"Know that in the section of this root there are many dispositions, for which reason it seems to me that it would be better to leave it alone."
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	"And I will tell you about the procedure and the symptoms of a boil."
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	"I say therefore that many boils come on the body, especially on the buttocks; and this happens often."
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	"This is to say that it is due to acid and watery humor that has spread to the buttocks, or from an injury;"
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	"and the color of the boil is according to the color of the skin; and it does not cause pain, yet it is a severe boil;"
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	"and sometimes there are painful and hard boils with a purplish color, and occasionally one comes from an artery or congestion of veins."
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	"When it is due to an artery, it is known by the hot disposition of the boil when you press it with your fingers;"
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	"And it is not necessary that you touch it."
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois,	"That which is caused by congestion of veins is known by its disposition when touched with the fingers,"
et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	"and can be treated in this manner and also on other parts."
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	"And it is that you cut the root of the buttocks, then raise the boil at the top and treat it with warm water and clean cloths, and relieve the suspension from all around the boil."
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	"If the boil is already solid with these nearby parts, then it is necessary that you treat the boil and cut it open;"
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	"And if it is hard to the touch or within the vessels, then it is necessary that you relieve all the tension and cut it completely around."
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	"And if the birthmark of the skin is in the hinder part, then it is necessary that you cut off all of it and remove the boil as we have said."
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And when your procedure is completed, then fill the wound with wool moistened in rose oil and wine, then dress it with other dressings until it is healed."
de l’aposteme des coions	"On boil on buttocks"
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a .i. borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions,	This is an abscess covered by a covering resembling a strawberry, with softening of the joints
et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	and the patient cries out in pain when he walks;
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant,	"And the treatment of this illness is almost as fearful as what came before."
et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	"However, we will tell you the operation for it according to what the ancients did."
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus .i. siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois,	"You must have the patient sit on one raised chair and then place a sling below their arms at your thighs,"
a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	"And take hold of the master's hand, extend it strongly;
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert,	"Then cut sharply and widely across the tendons on the outer side of the wrist until they are exposed,"
et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	"And then scrape away from each side as we have said in the extraction of the arteries that are in the temples;"
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	"Then I will insert a needle with a doubled thread and tie it at the first place where the nerve appeared, and then tie it again at the other end;"
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	"Then cut through it evenly along the length of the body, and remove the corrupted tissues;"
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	"And then dress the wound as is done for other operations where sinews are cut, so that no blood vessels nourish either of the tendons;"
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	"For otherwise there will be no harm, and if the nerve comes from all the vessels, then it is necessary to tie the tendons to all the vessels;"
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	"So that the bone does not lose its nourishment due to the incision of the vessels, and they dry up and cannot heal."
de la routure dou syfac	"Treatment for a broken nose:"
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	"The outcome of this condition depends on whether the fracture reaches the nasal septum or extends onto the frontal bone in the angle region. If it does not reach the nasal septum, then the intestines descend from that side of the nose;"
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces .ij. manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	"And this fracture occurs either in the nasal bone itself or due to an extension of it, and these two types arise from many causes such as blows, falls, jumps, carrying heavy weights, and similar incidents;"
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	"The signs that it is an extension of the nasal bone fracture are that it occurs gradually over a long period and does not happen suddenly;"
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	"And there is swelling all around towards the back, because the nasal bone presses on the intestines."
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	"And the signs that it is a fracture of the nasal bone itself are that there is sudden pain at the onset, and there is diverse swelling apparent under the skin, due to the escape of intestinal contents through the defect in the nasal bone."
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	"And sometimes the intestines may descend with the fracture and become trapped in it, causing great pain to the patient, especially when they are pressed upon."
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	"And these fractures of the nasal bone require careful handling so that they do not happen frequently due to poor treatment."
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	"The method of treatment is as follows: you should instruct the patient to gently replace any prolapsed intestines back into the wound using their hand if possible;"
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	"Then elevate his head between your hands and raise his thighs;"
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	"Then elevate the heart above (the level of) the wound and cut away all the skin from the tendons along their length;"
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	"Then insert bone forceps into the wound near the nasal bone using however many you need to expose the fracture and allow the bone to protrude;"
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	"Then strip away the periosteum covering the nasal bone until it is exposed on all sides;"
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac,	"Then insert your index finger into the opening at the base of the tendon, between the two nasal bones and behind the upper lip;"
et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	"And separate the tissue behind the upper lip and between the two nasal bones. Then use your right hand to elevate the tendon from inside the wound while using your left hand to expose the nasal bone and lift up the upper lip together with the nasal bone towards the neck;"
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	"And instruct your assistant to elevate the upper lip while releasing any tension behind it;"
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	"Then check with both hands whether there is any prolapsed intestine wrapped around the nasal bone. If you find any, push it back into the abdominal cavity;"
puis pren une aguille ou il ait .i. gros fil fait de .x. filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait .iiij. filz;	"Then take a needle with a thread made of 10 strands and insert it into the posterior aspect of the nasal bone behind the tendon. Then cut off the excess thread leaving about 4 inches;"
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de .ij. pars;	"Then tie the threads together in a cross-over fashion and secure the nasal bone (which is underneath the tendon) with a strong knot tied twice;"
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de .ij. pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	"Then wrap the threads around the nasal bone and tie them securely with two knots to prevent any vessels that supply it from entering the wound and causing swelling;"
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc .ij. dois de celui, et aprés ces .ij. liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	"Then place the second knot in line with the first knot about two fingers' width away from it. After tying these knots, leave enough length of nasal bone underneath the tendon to protrude a finger's width;"
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	"And then trim the excess nasal bone flush with the curvature of the upper lip. Then cut away any remaining skin and muscle from underneath the tendon as described earlier;"
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	"Then apply moistened lint soaked in oil to the wound and secure it with the knot we have described."
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	"And sometimes it may be necessary to cauterize the exposed nasal bone after the incision has been made in case of any bleeding."
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	"For this happens very often and leaves the knot hanging loose. If it takes too long to fall off, it should be removed with warm water and the dressing reapplied until it does fall off;"
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	"Then treat the wound using other methods until it heals perfectly."
de hernie carnouse	Here is the translation of the given text with a focus on the term "hernie carnosous":
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this art I have never seen anyone dare to perform a cure by iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is done in such a way as one sees the art together, so that you bind the vessels, after cutting it lightly above or below.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then cut off the head of the shoulder, and cure the wound that caused it until the vessels bleed; and cure it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	Sometimes a rupture occurs in the angles, as we have said, and the place is opened; and none of the intestines come out of their places, except for a little bit, which should be repaired immediately.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	And if it remains too long at this point, the wound swells or becomes infected until the intestines come out.
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	And this happens due to the expansion of the infection that is at the angles, as we have said, because it is expanded, then the place becomes softened and swollen and opened.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	And the cure for this is by cauterization, as we have said before; and sometimes it is cured with iron in this way:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de .iij. dois;	And that the sick person lies on their back between your hands, then cut off the swollen place of the rupture from its width according to the quantity of three fingers;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	And then remove the infection that is under the skin where it entered, then take a hot iron and place it on the visible place of the infection;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les .ij. leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	And press it to the depth of the belly, then cut the two visible places of the infection on top of the iron, and cut both of them.
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	Then remove the top of the iron, and do not cut into the infection or extend it with any other thing, as I have told you in the treatment of intestinal prolapse.
puis le cure par la cure des plaies. Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	Then heal it according to the treatment for wounds. And when you cut the threads, cleanse and heal the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The infection is confined, and has no appearance in the rupture, and the cauterization should be performed more gently at this place, and closer to saving the patient's life.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	Regarding the softening of the skin of the thighs
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Many times the skin of the thighs becomes softened in some men because the flesh that is inside is softened, and it is unpleasant to see. And it is necessary, when one wants to heal it, for the sick person to lie on their back, and cut off the softened skin from the natural skin; then join the two lips with a suture, and if you wish, first sew up the excess of the softened skin with three or four stitches firmly; then cut between the sutures, and heal it as one would other wounds until it is healed, and remove the thread.
dou chastrement	Regarding castration
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por .ij. manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes. Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc .ij. manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.  En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.  Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a .i. cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Know that castrations are forbidden in our law, and I would like not to speak of it in this book. And there is no need to mention it except for two reasons: the first is that the surgeon should know how to respond when asked about it and its treatment; the second is because we often have a need to castrate certain animals to help us, such as goats, sheep, cats, and other animals. I say therefore that castrations are performed in two ways: either by traction or by cutting. In the one that we perform by traction, we make the animal sit in hot water until the testicles are softened and hanging, then grasp them with your hand until they are relaxed and you no longer feel them. For castration by cutting: it is necessary to tie the animal, press the skin of the testicles with your left hand, then tie the suspensiony ligament, and cut each testicle with one cut after having well scraped them; leave a little piece of skin around the wound and remove the delicate tissue that is on the vessels; this manner of castration is gentle compared to that done by traction because sometimes some things remain at the traction which causes the animal to desire lust, then heal the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	Regarding hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc .ij. manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les .ij. coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.  Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et .ij. coions.  Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	Hermaphroditism occurs in two ways among men: one way is that between the two testicles opens also like the figure of a woman's nature, or it has hair, and sometimes urine comes out from there. And the other way among women is to have on the pubic area both a penis and two testicles. The treatment for the man and the woman is to cut away all the attached skin and treat it as other wounds; in the second way, for men whose urine flows through the skin of the testicles, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	Tenting
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure. Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee». Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	Tenting is an attachment on the natural part that is too ugly to look at; some women have it as large as a hand, and that is its treatment. You must cut away the superfluous growth of the tenting with your hand or scissors, cutting it lightly; do not go too deep, lest blood flow, then treat it like any other wound until it is healed; and there is another growth that appears at the mouth of the womb, and the anus, sometimes urine flows out, and resembles the likeness of a cow, and for this reason the ancients called it «cow disease». You must cut it away, as we have said with tenting, and treat it until it is healed.
de erratique	Erratique
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile. Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait. S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as .ij. leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes .ij. dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les .ij. leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder. Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte. Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef; puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec; puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.  Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez. Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	Erratique is when the nature of woman is not pierced or the opening is small; it is either natural at birth or accidental due to illness that has occurred there; or it is from attached skin, or thin and subtle mucous membrane or thick, and is located deep in the womb or on the sides or below where it may be; and it prevents conception and childbirth, and sometimes also the flow of menstrual blood; and its recognition is by the appearance of the vaginal opening. If the obstruction is close at hand, then try with your fingers or a probe to reach it.
